<ins class="adsbygoogle" style="display:block" data-ad-client="ca-pub-8347943306296683" data-ad-slot="1400453447" data-ad-format="auto" data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins> <script type="litespeed/javascript">(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({})</script></div><p>The <strong>2025 ICC Champions Trophy start date</strong> is <strong>February 19th</strong>, and the tournament will run until <strong>March 9th, 2025</strong>. Pakistan will host the International Cricket Council (ICC) Champions Trophy, a cricket tournament for the eight best-ranked men’s national teams in One Day Internationals (ODIs). Pakistan is the current defending champion, having won the 2017 edition.</p><h2 class="kt-adv-heading681_6a12bf-3f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-1-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_6a12bf-3f"><strong>ICC Champions Trophy 2025</strong> Schedule Team List Venue</h2><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id681_714584-80 alignfull has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kb-theme-content-width"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column681_afc14d-4e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="wp-block-kadence-posts kb-posts kb-posts-id-681_c4bc4a-24 content-wrap grid-cols kb-posts-style-boxed grid-sm-col-1 grid-lg-col-1 item-image-style-above"><article class="entry content-bg loop-entry post-5370 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-news-updates tag-icc-champions-trophy-2025 tag-india-vs-pakistan">

block; clear: both;"> <script type="litespeed/javascript" data-src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-8347943306296683" ></script> 
<ins class="adsbygoogle" style="display:block" data-ad-client="ca-pub-8347943306296683" data-ad-slot="5972993974" data-ad-format="auto" data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins> <script type="litespeed/javascript">(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({})</script></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_5cb074-0f"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div><h3 class="kt-adv-heading681_e80f66-c9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-1-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_e80f66-c9"><strong>History of the ICC Champions Trophy</strong></h3><p class="kt-adv-heading681_8889a4-58 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_8889a4-58">The <strong>ICC Champions Trophy</strong> is a special cricket tournament. It started to make <strong>ODI cricket</strong> popular and bring the best cricket teams in the world together to play exciting matches. The first tournament happened in 1998 in <strong>Dhaka, Bangladesh</strong>. <strong>South Africa</strong> won that first tournament, beating the <strong>West Indies</strong> in the final match.</p><p class="has-text-align-left">In the beginning, the tournament was simple: if a team lost, they went home! But later, the tournament changed and became bigger, with teams playing in groups before the knockout matches. In 2002, the name became the <strong>ICC Champions Trophy</strong>, and something unusual happened: <strong>India and Sri Lanka</strong> both became winners together because rain stopped the final match twice in <strong>Colombo</strong>.</p><p class="has-text-align-left">The tournament kept getting better and more thrilling. <strong>Australia</strong> was the first team to win two times in a row, in 2006 and 2009, showing how strong they were. In 2004, the <strong>West Indies</strong> beat <strong>England</strong> in an exciting match to win. In 2013, <strong>India</strong> won again by defeating England in a final that was shortened because of rain. Then, in 2017, something amazing happened: <strong>Pakistan</strong> beat their rivals <strong>India</strong> to win their first-ever Champions Trophy!</p><p class="has-text-align-left">The ICC Champions Trophy 2017 was in <strong>England</strong>. <strong>Pakistan</strong> played brilliantly, even though they started as the lowest-ranked team. In the final, they beat <strong>India</strong> by 180 runs at <strong>The Oval</strong>, a huge victory that showed how strong Pakistan could be in cricket! <a href="history-of-icc-champions-trophy/" data-type="link" data-id="https://championstrophy2025.com/history-of-icc-champions-trophy/">read more</a></p><div class="code-block code-block-4" style="margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;"> <script type="litespeed/javascript" data-src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-8347943306296683" ></script> 
<ins class="adsbygoogle" style="display:block" data-ad-client="ca-pub-8347943306296683" data-ad-slot="1400453447" data-ad-format="auto" data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins> <script type="litespeed/javascript">(adsbygoogle=window.adsbygoogle||[]).push({})</script></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_f290fa-04"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div></div></div></div></div><h2 class="kt-adv-heading681_396d46-7e wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-1-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_396d46-7e"><strong>ICC Champions Trophy 2025 Schedule</strong></h2><div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_338d48-a7"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div><p>The <a href="tag/icc-champions-trophy-schedule/">ICC has released the 2025 Champions Trophy schedule</a>, which will take place in Pakistan from February 19 to March 9. Matches venue will be in Karachi, Lahore Rawalpindi and Dubai. <strong>Group A includes Pakistan, India, New Zealand, and Bangladesh</strong>, while <strong>Group B features Australia, England, Afghanistan, and South Africa</strong>.</p><figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-fixed-layout"><thead><tr><th class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Date</th><th class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Match</th><th class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Venue</th><th>Details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">19 Feb 2025</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Opening Ceremony</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Karachi</td><td>Likely to feature the inaugural match between Pakistan and New Zealand.</td></tr><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">20 Feb 2025</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Bangladesh vs. India</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">Dubai</td><td>India’s first group-stage match.</td></tr><tr><td class="has-text-align-center" class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_d2a9d5-e9"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div><h2 class="kt-adv-heading681_bad30a-79 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-1-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_bad30a-79"><strong>Champions Trophy 2025 – Updates and Developments</strong></h2><p>The ICC Champions Trophy 2025 is scheduled from February 19 to March 9, 2025. Initially, Pakistan was set to host the tournament, with matches planned in Karachi, Lahore, and Rawalpindi. However, due to security concerns raised by India, the tournament’s venue has been adjusted.</p><p>Under the &#8220;<a href="hybrid-model-in-cricket/" data-type="link" data-id="https://championstrophy2025.com/hybrid-model-in-cricket/"><strong>hybrid model</strong></a>,&#8221; the tournament will be co-hosted by Pakistan and the United Arab Emirates (UAE). Matches involving India will be played in Dubai, while other matches, including those featuring Pakistan, will take place in Pakistan. This arrangement aims to accommodate India’s security concerns while allowing Pakistan to showcase its cricketing venues.</p><p>The tournament will feature matches in both countries, with the final decision on the venue for the semi-finals and final to be determined based on team qualifications.<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2025_ICC_Champions_Trophy" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow"></a></p><p>For more detailed news and developments about the ICC Champions Trophy 2025, check out the <strong><a href="latest-news-updates/">Latest News Updates</a></strong>.</p><div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_359525-e2"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div><h3 class="kt-adv-heading681_26f71c-bf wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-1-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_26f71c-bf"><strong>The Format of the 2025 ICC Champions Trophy</strong></h3><p>The <strong>Champions Trophy 2025</strong> will have a similar format to the past years. It will include the <strong>top eight ODI teams</strong> from around the world. These teams will compete in a fun and exciting tournament!</p><ol class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Group Stage</strong>: The teams are divided into <strong>two groups of four</strong>. Each team will play <strong>three matches</strong> against other teams in their group.</li><li><strong>Knockout Stage</strong>: The <strong>top two teams</strong> from each group will move to the <strong>semi-finals</strong>. The winners of the semi-finals will then play in the <strong>grand final</strong> to see who is the best!</li></ol><p>This setup makes sure that all teams play <strong>at least three matches</strong>, so we get to see how strong and consistent each team is. It also makes the tournament very exciting, with only the best teams reaching the final matches!</p><h3 class="kt-adv-heading681_5cdabf-ca wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_5cdabf-ca"><strong>Teams to Watch in 2025</strong></h3><p>Many cricket teams will try to win the <strong>Champions Trophy 2025</strong>. Some of the strongest teams are <strong>India</strong>, <strong>Australia</strong>, <strong>England</strong>, and <strong>Pakistan</strong>.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>India</strong> is always very good in big cricket tournaments. They really want to win this time because they came very close in 2017 but didn’t get the trophy.</li><li><strong>Australia</strong> is amazing at playing white-ball cricket. They have won the <strong>Champions Trophy</strong> two times before and will try hard to win their third one.</li><li><strong>England</strong> won the 2019 World Cup and are now one of the best teams in the world. They became much better with their captain, Eoin Morgan, and are very strong in short cricket matches.</li><li><strong>Pakistan</strong> won the last <strong>Champions Trophy</strong> in 2017. They will want to win again, especially if the tournament happens in Pakistan!</li></ul><p>Other teams like <strong>New Zealand</strong> are always tough in ICC tournaments. The <strong>West Indies</strong> have already won the <strong>Champions Trophy</strong> two times and could be dangerous again. <strong>South Africa</strong> wants to do well this time. They won the first <strong>Champions Trophy</strong> in 1998, but they haven’t been lucky in recent years.</p><p>All these teams will fight hard to be champions!</p><div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_7f1012-a8"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id681_5467f0-a3 alignfull has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column681_e35b62-1e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="kt-adv-heading681_566a37-b3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-1-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_566a37-b3"><strong>2025 Champions Trophy Teams</strong></h2><div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-681_d36f3b-4c"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div><p>The <strong>Champions Trophy 2025</strong> is a big and exciting cricket tournament where the <a href="teams/" data-type="link" data-id="https://championstrophy2025.com/teams/">best 8 teams</a> in the world will play to win the special title. The teams are split into two groups:</p><div class="code-block code-block-5" style="margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;"> <script type="litespeed/javascript" data-src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-8347943306296683" ></script>

People are very excited to see which country will host the tournament. It might be played in <strong>Pakistan</strong>, or it could be moved to a different, neutral place.</p><p>The <strong>Champions Trophy</strong> has a long history full of amazing matches, famous players, and exciting moments. The year 2025 will bring more great cricket games, with lots of fun and competition. Fans are ready to cheer for their favorite teams and see the best of <strong>ODI cricket</strong>!</p><p class="has-text-align-left">As the hosts, Pakistan were automatically qualified to participate. Seven of the other top-ranked teams from the group stage of the 2023 Cricket World Cup also participated. For the first time ever, reigning champions Sri Lanka did not make the cut, and this tournament will be Afghanistan’s maiden debut.</p><figure class="wp-block-table alignwide is-style-regular"><table class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What is the ICC Men’s Champions Trophy?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_881201-02 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_881201-02">The ICC Men’s Champions Trophy is a quadrennial One Day International (ODI) cricket tournament organized by the International Cricket Council (ICC). It features the top eight ranked ODI teams in the world. The tournament is often referred to as the &#8220;Mini World Cup&#8221; due to its format and the participation of all top cricketing nations.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane681_cab8d5-80"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">When and where will the 2025 Champions Trophy be held?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_e76146-e2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_e76146-e2">The 2025 ICC Men’s Champions Trophy will be hosted by Pakistan from February 19 to March 9, 2025.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane681_610f50-57"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">How do teams qualify for the Champions Trophy?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_f3bf60-3e wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_f3bf60-3e">Starting with the 2025 tournament, the top eight teams from the most recent Cricket World Cup automatically qualify for the Champions Trophy. This replaces the previous qualification process which was based on ICC ODI rankings.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-4 kt-pane681_1ddc84-2b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Why was the Champions Trophy originally discontinued?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_a5996a-2c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_a5996a-2c">In 2016, the ICC decided to cancel future editions of the Champions Trophy after the 2017 tournament. This was done with the intention of having only one major tournament for each format of international cricket. However, the tournament was later reinstated.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-5 kt-pane681_d81997-2c"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What is the format of the Champions Trophy?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_1d46c6-10 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_1d46c6-10">Eight teams are divided into two groups of four. Each team plays every other team in their group in a round-robin format. The top two teams from each group advance to the semi-finals. The winners of the semi-finals then play in the final to determine the champion.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-6 kt-pane681_43cab6-4e"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What are the proposed venues for the 2025 Champions Trophy?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_765fe2-6c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_765fe2-6c">The Pakistan Cricket Board (PCB) has proposed three venues for the tournament: Karachi, Lahore, and Rawalpindi. However, with India’s withdrawal, the final venues and schedule are yet to be confirmed.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-7 kt-pane681_60f782-1c"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Is there a Trophy Tour happening before the tournament?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_8b1917-c9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_8b1917-c9">Yes, the ICC has announced a global Trophy Tour in partnership with DP World. It will start in Islamabad, Pakistan, visiting major cities across all eight participating nations, including Afghanistan, Bangladesh, South Africa, Australia, New Zealand, England, and India, before returning to Pakistan for the tournament.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-8 kt-pane681_d1aa27-0b"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Is India participating in the 2025 Champions Trophy?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p class="kt-adv-heading681_d7d9f1-f8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading681_d7d9f1-f8">Till today 24-November-2024 No, India has announced that they will not travel to Pakistan for the 2025 Champions Trophy due to security concerns and disapproval from their government. This has created uncertainty over the tournament’s schedule and venue plans.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><p></p><hr/><p><strong><em><span style="color: #000000;">Check out the <a title="Champions Trophy 2025 Schedule" href="icc-champions-trophy-2025-schedule/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Champions Trophy Schedule</a>, <a href="live-score/"
